When matched, clears the entire column it is on.\r\n✓ By connecting 10-11 diamonds of the same color you get a cross buster. When matched, clears the entire row and column it is on.\r\n✓ If you are able to match more than 11 diamonds, you get a super diamond. This can be grouped with any other single diamond on the board. When activated, all the same-colored diamonds as the diamond it was matched with, will be removed from the board.\r\n✓ By connecting 5 diamonds of the same color you get a joker diamond.
